<h3 align="center" tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-bootstrap" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#bootstrap"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Bootstrap</h3>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  Sleek, intuitive, and powerful front-end framework for faster and easier web development.
  <br>
  <a href="https://getbootstrap.com/docs/5.3/" rel="nofollow"><strong>Explore Bootstrap docs »</strong></a>
  <br>
  <br>
  <a href="https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/issues/new?assignees=-&amp;labels=bug&amp;template=bug_report.yml">Report bug</a>
  ·
  <a href="https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/issues/new?assignees=&amp;labels=feature&amp;template=feature_request.yml">Request feature</a>
  ·
  <a href="https://themes.getbootstrap.com/" rel="nofollow">Themes</a>
  ·
  <a href="https://blog.getbootstrap.com/" rel="nofollow">Blog</a>
</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-bootstrap-5" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#bootstrap-5"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Bootstrap 5</h2>
<p dir="auto">Our default branch is for development of our Bootstrap 5 release. Head to the <a href="https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/tree/v4-dev"><code>v4-dev</code> branch</a> to view the readme, documentation, and source code for Bootstrap 4.</p>

<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-quick-start" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#quick-start"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Quick start</h2>
<p dir="auto">Several quick start options are available:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/archive/v5.3.2.zip">Download the latest release</a></li>
<li>Clone the repo: <code>git clone https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap.git</code></li>
<li>Install with <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/" rel="nofollow">npm</a>: <code>npm install bootstrap@v5.3.2</code></li>
<li>Install with <a href="https://yarnpkg.com/" rel="nofollow">yarn</a>: <code>yarn add bootstrap@v5.3.2</code></li>
<li>Install with <a href="https://getcomposer.org/" rel="nofollow">Composer</a>: <code>composer require twbs/bootstrap:5.3.2</code></li>
<li>Install with <a href="https://www.nuget.org/" rel="nofollow">NuGet</a>: CSS: <code>Install-Package bootstrap</code> Sass: <code>Install-Package bootstrap.sass</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Read the <a href="https://getbootstrap.com/docs/5.3/getting-started/introduction/" rel="nofollow">Getting started page</a> for information on the framework contents, templates, examples, and more.</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-status" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#status"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Status</h2>

<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-whats-included" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#whats-included"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>What's included</h2>
<p dir="auto">Within the download you'll find the following directories and files, logically grouping common assets and providing both compiled and minified variations.</p>

<p dir="auto">We provide compiled CSS and JS (<code>bootstrap.*</code>), as well as compiled and minified CSS and JS (<code>bootstrap.min.*</code>). <a href="https://developers.google.com/web/tools/chrome-devtools/javascript/source-maps" rel="nofollow">Source maps</a> (<code>bootstrap.*.map</code>) are available for use with certain browsers' developer tools. Bundled JS files (<code>bootstrap.bundle.js</code> and minified <code>bootstrap.bundle.min.js</code>) include <a href="https://popper.js.org/" rel="nofollow">Popper</a>.</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-bugs-and-feature-requests" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#bugs-and-feature-requests"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Bugs and feature requests</h2>
<p dir="auto">Have a bug or a feature request? Please first read the <a href="https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/blob/main/.github/CONTRIBUTING.md#using-the-issue-tracker">issue guidelines</a> and search for existing and closed issues. If your problem or idea is not addressed yet, <a href="https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/issues/new/choose">please open a new issue</a>.</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-documentation" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#documentation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Documentation</h2>
<p dir="auto">Bootstrap's documentation, included in this repo in the root directory, is built with <a href="https://gohugo.io/" rel="nofollow">Hugo</a> and publicly hosted on GitHub Pages at <a href="https://getbootstrap.com/" rel="nofollow">https://getbootstrap.com/</a>. The docs may also be run locally.</p>
<p dir="auto">Documentation search is powered by <a href="https://docsearch.algolia.com/" rel="nofollow">Algolia's DocSearch</a>.</p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-running-documentation-locally" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#running-documentation-locally"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Running documentation locally</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Run <code>npm install</code> to install the Node.js dependencies, including Hugo (the site builder).</li>
<li>Run <code>npm run test</code> (or a specific npm script) to rebuild distributed CSS and JavaScript files, as well as our docs assets.</li>
<li>From the root <code>/bootstrap</code> directory, run <code>npm run docs-serve</code> in the command line.</li>
<li>Open <code>http://localhost:9001/</code> in your browser, and voilà.</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">Learn more about using Hugo by reading its <a href="https://gohugo.io/documentation/" rel="nofollow">documentation</a>.</p>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-documentation-for-previous-releases" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#documentation-for-previous-releases"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Documentation for previous releases</h3>
<p dir="auto">You can find all our previous releases docs on <a href="https://getbootstrap.com/docs/versions/" rel="nofollow">https://getbootstrap.com/docs/versions/</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/releases">Previous releases</a> and their documentation are also available for download.</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-contributing" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#contributing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Contributing</h2>
<p dir="auto">Please read through our <a href="https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/blob/main/.github/CONTRIBUTING.md">contributing guidelines</a>. Included are directions for opening issues, coding standards, and notes on development.</p>
<p dir="auto">Moreover, if your pull request contains JavaScript patches or features, you must include <a href="https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/tree/main/js/tests">relevant unit tests</a>. All HTML and CSS should conform to the <a href="https://github.com/mdo/code-guide">Code Guide</a>, maintained by <a href="https://github.com/mdo">Mark Otto</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Editor preferences are available in the <a href="https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/blob/main/.editorconfig">editor config</a> for easy use in common text editors. Read more and download plugins at <a href="https://editorconfig.org/" rel="nofollow">https://editorconfig.org/</a>.</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-community" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#community"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Community</h2>
<p dir="auto">Get updates on Bootstrap's development and chat with the project maintainers and community members.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Follow <a href="https://twitter.com/getbootstrap" rel="nofollow">@getbootstrap on Twitter</a>.</li>
<li>Read and subscribe to <a href="https://blog.getbootstrap.com/" rel="nofollow">The Official Bootstrap Blog</a>.</li>
<li>Ask questions and explore <a href="https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/discussions">our GitHub Discussions</a>.</li>
<li>Discuss, ask questions, and more on <a href="https://discord.gg/bZUvakRU3M" rel="nofollow">the community Discord</a> or <a href="https://reddit.com/r/bootstrap" rel="nofollow">Bootstrap subreddit</a>.</li>
<li>Chat with fellow Bootstrappers in IRC. On the <code>irc.libera.chat</code> server, in the <code>#bootstrap</code> channel.</li>
<li>Implementation help may be found at Stack Overflow (tagged <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/bootstrap-5" rel="nofollow"><code>bootstrap-5</code></a>).</li>
<li>Developers should use the keyword <code>bootstrap</code> on packages which modify or add to the functionality of Bootstrap when distributing through <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/browse/keyword/bootstrap" rel="nofollow">npm</a> or similar delivery mechanisms for maximum discoverability.</li>
</ul>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-versioning" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#versioning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Versioning</h2>
<p dir="auto">For transparency into our release cycle and in striving to maintain backward compatibility, Bootstrap is maintained under <a href="https://semver.org/" rel="nofollow">the Semantic Versioning guidelines</a>. Sometimes we screw up, but we adhere to those rules whenever possible.</p>
<p dir="auto">See <a href="https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/releases">the Releases section of our GitHub project</a> for changelogs for each release version of Bootstrap. Release announcement posts on <a href="https://blog.getbootstrap.com/" rel="nofollow">the official Bootstrap blog</a> contain summaries of the most noteworthy changes made in each release.</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-creators" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#creators"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Creators</h2>
